It comes in your choice between LE, XLE, and Limited trim levels, each equipped with a 144-horsepower 4-cylinder engine. All-wheel drive is not available, and, if you&rsquo;re wondering, C-HR stands for &ldquo;Coupe, High-Roof.&rdquo;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003ELearn more about the \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.jdpower.com\u002Fcars\u002Fshopping-guides\u002Ftop-10-2020-small-suvs-by-customer-satisfaction?make=&amp;model=\"\u003ETop 10 2020 Small SUVs in Overall Appeal\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E","fastFact":"","modelId":"0","styleId":"0","studyName":"","featured":"1"},{"articleId":"5554","abstract":"Aside from filling the gas tank, changing a cars engine oil is perhaps the most common task required to keep a vehicle running properly. Fresh oil is an engines best friend, but too much of it can cause costly damage. Learn what happens when you put too much oil in your car.","year":"","make":"","model":"","title":"What Happens When You Put Too Much Oil in Your Car?","subtitle":"What Happens When You Put Too Much Oil in Your Car?","img":"https:\u002F\u002Fcdn.jdpower.com\u002Fchanging-oil.jpg","bodyStyle":"N\u002FA","postDate":"2020-04-16T17:58:00.000Z","contentType":"Misc","articleName":"What Happens When You Put Too Much Oil in Your Car?","contributor":"Thom Blackett","path":"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.jdpower.com\u002Fcars\u002Fshopping-guides\u002Fwhat-happens-when-you-put-too-much-oil-in-your-car","shortPath":"what-happens-when-you-put-too-much-oil-in-your-car","body":"\u003Cp\u003EAside from filling the gas tank, changing a car&rsquo;s engine oil is perhaps the most common task required to keep a vehicle running properly. This bit of routine maintenance can be done by a quick-lube station during your lunch break, at the dealership while running errands on a Saturday morning, or even in your own driveway after work. Fresh oil is an engine&rsquo;s best friend, but too much of it can cause costly damage and should be removed as soon as possible.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cimg alt=\"What Happens When You Put Too Much Oil in Your Car?\" src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fcdn.jdpower.com\u002Fchanging-oil.jpg\" \u002F\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EDangers of Overfilling the Engine Oil\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003ETo understand how overfilling your engine oil is too much of a good thing, it&rsquo;s helpful to first provide a little background.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EEngines are comprised of hundreds of precision-crafted parts working in unison at high speeds and temperatures, all of which require oil for proper lubrication and smooth movement. You, or your mechanic, add oil to an engine to the crankcase via the cap labeled &ldquo;Oil&rdquo; under the hood. The oil settles in the oil pan when the engine is not running. When you start the engine, the oil circulates throughout the engine and passes through an oil filter that removes contaminants that could potentially cause damage.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EWhen too much oil is added, the level in the oil pan becomes too high. That allows a fast-moving lobed rod called the crankshaft to come into contact with the oil and essentially aerate it. The result is a foamy, frothy substance that cannot properly lubricate the engine. Think of this as your engine&rsquo;s way of turning cream into whipped cream. No one wants whipped cream lubricating their engine.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EAlso of concern, the extra oil creates excessive pressure inside your engine that will look for an escape through various gaskets and seals. If one or more of those fail, that will lead to leaks and costly repairs.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EPotential Causes of Excess Oil in Your Engine\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003EWhen investigating why there&rsquo;s too much oil in your engine, there&rsquo;s one blatantly obvious answer: either you or your mechanic overfilled the crankcase when topping off or after an oil change. Along those same lines, failing to properly drain old engine oil when doing an oil change, or adding too much oil to the new filter, could also be the culprits.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EIf those simple mistakes didn&rsquo;t cause the problem, you may find that the extra &ldquo;oil&rdquo; is actually a combination of fluids. Condensation can build up inside an engine, fuel can get past a faulty seal, or a failing head gasket can allow coolant to leak. In any of these scenarios, you&rsquo;ll have an excess of diluted oil that can cause serious damage.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EHow to Determine if Your Engine Has Too Much Oil\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003EIf you suspect you have too much oil in your engine, the quickest way to get an answer is to look at the dipstick. With the exception of some high-end exotic models, this simple part is found in all \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.jdpower.com\u002Fcars\u002Fbody-styles\"\u003Etypes of cars\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, typically has a bright yellow pull handle, and features low and high marks to show if your car has too much, too little, or the perfect amount of oil. It&rsquo;s advisable to get into the habit of checking the level frequently, and always after an oil change. Consult your owner&rsquo;s manual for specific guidance on checking your car&rsquo;s dipstick.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThere are other indicators that will suggest you have an overfill problem, including blue exhaust smoke, a burning smell, an oil leak, or a high reading on your oil pressure gauge (if equipped). If the engine is running rough or your check engine light illuminates, the cause may be excess oil contacting the spark plugs and causing a misfire.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EHow to Remove Excess Oil from Your Engine\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003ESome backyard mechanics suggest siphoning excess engine oil from the dipstick or crankcase cap, but we recommend a safer and more precise method. Perform a fresh oil change.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EIf you&rsquo;re comfortable doing your own oil change, you&rsquo;ll remove the oil drain plug at the bottom of the oil pan, completely drain the engine of oil, remove and replace the oil filter, and refill the oil with the proper amount specified in your owner&rsquo;s manual. Naturally, you&rsquo;ll need a drain container to collect the oil and dispose of it properly (local recycling centers and auto parts stores usually charge a small fee to accept used oil). Also, remember that if you&rsquo;ve been driving the car before the oil change, the oil is likely hot and could cause burns if you don&rsquo;t handle it appropriately.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EIf you would rather have this service completed by a mechanic, consider having the car towed to the repair shop to avoid possibly causing engine damage during the trip.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003ECompare Cars Before You Buy\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003EOperating an engine with excess oil can lead to costly repairs. This, along with an economy stifled by business shutdowns and restrictions, has prompted many people to sell their current vehicle and\u002For downsize their family vehicle fleet. Some consumers are also trading a larger or luxury vehicle for a smaller non-luxury vehicle that is less expensive to own and operate.&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EOn the other hand, the desire by many to avoid the use of public transportation has spurred former bus, train, and subway riders to purchase a car. The prospect of sharing a ride in close proximity with dozens of other passengers just doesn&#39;t seem palatable right now.&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EWhat this means is lots of people are buying and selling used cars. This is attested to by statistics on used car sales at auction gathered by J.D. Power. Of course, if you&#39;re going to do that, you have many options. Some are obvious, like trading the car in or selling it to a neighbor or friend, and some are less obvious, like selling it to a national used car retailer or getting a guaranteed price from a local dealer. The vehicle&#39;s model year, brand, model, mileage, and overall condition are key factors in determining what it is worth.&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EHappily, there is a free resource that takes all the necessary factors into account. Included among them are rough, average, and clean trade-in values (based on vehicle condition), the &quot;clean retail&quot; value, and a certified pre-owned value.&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EIf you plan to trade your car in as you purchase a new vehicle you can expect to receive the appropriate trade-in value. With that in mind, TSS 2.0 consists of an array of active safety features that share the same goal &mdash; eliminate as many accidents as possible and mitigate the effects of accidents that are impossible to prevent.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EIn an effort to accomplish those lofty goals, Toyota Safety Sense 2.0 is engineered to enhance driver awareness, decision-making, and vehicle operation over a wide range of speeds and conditions. Among its key benefits, TSS 2.0 is an integrated system whose total abilities go beyond the sum of its individual parts. They join previously available TSS features including adaptive cruise control, forward collision warning, automatic emergency braking, lane departure warning with lane keeping assistance, and automatic high-beam headlights.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EShould the forward collision warning system determine that there is a high possibility of a frontal collision, it warns the driver to take evasive action and to brake with both audible and visual warning. If the driver applies the brakes too gently, the system can automatically provide additional braking force. The system may also automatically apply the brakes if the driver doesn&#39;t respond to the warnings. In low-light situations, the system can sense vehicles and pedestrians, and it can detect bicyclists in normal daylight, providing warnings and then automatically braking if situations warrant.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EAdaptive cruise control, which Toyota calls Dynamic Radar Cruise Control (DRCC), enables drivers to automatically maintain a set speed and set interval from the vehicle ahead. If it detects that the preceding vehicle is traveling at a slower speed it will slow the Toyota to maintain the established following distance, and it can do so to a complete stop. If the preceding vehicle speeds up, DRCC will accelerate back to your set speed.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003ETSS 2.0&#39;s lane departure warning and lane keeping assistance system (Lane Departure Alert, or LDA) features both steering assist and road edge detection. If the system senses the vehicle is starting to unintentionally deviate from its lane, it alerts the driver with an audible and visual warning. The system may also automatically make corrective steering inputs to help the driver keep the vehicle in its lane. Road Edge Detection is designed to sense the edge of the road surface to keep the vehicle on the pavement.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003ELane centering assistance (Lane Tracing Assist) works with DRCC to keep the vehicle centered in its marked lane to avoid unintended lane departures. This is not intended for semi-autonomous driving, however, and the driver must continue to hold the steering wheel.&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EAutomatic high-beam assistance helps the driver see better at night while reducing glare for other drivers. Virtually all of the sensing is done by a forward-facing single-lens camera and millimeter-wave radar. The in-vehicle camera does things that include detecting oncoming vehicles, determining lane markers and the road&#39;s edges, reading road signs, and sensing the presence of pedestrians and bicyclists. The radar helps detect vehicles, objects, and people in low-light situations and helps determine vehicle speed and the interval between the vehicle and the car that is preceding it.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EBecause TSS 2.0 is designed as an integrated system, each piece can perform multiple tasks, making its operation quicker and more cost-effective. Beyond camera and radar, the key component is its &quot;electronic brain,&quot; the computer processor that crunches the incoming data to draw conclusions that can help the driver. And it does all this constantly in milliseconds.&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EWith TSS 2.0, Toyota vehicles have one of the most functional and well-integrated driver safety systems in the world. Versus both previous versions of TSS and systems from competitive automakers, Toyota Safety Sense 2.0 represents a clear improvement in smoothness, sophistication, and accuracy.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cem\u003EThe information in this article is from Toyota and the author&rsquo;s experience with TSS 2.0. The technology learns your habits and preferences over time and responds to natural voice queries similar to smartphone assistants like Siri and smart home assistants like Amazon Alexa. Prompt the system with &ldquo;Hey, Mercedes&rdquo; and follow-up with a request.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EFor example, you could say: &ldquo;Hey, Mercedes, I want some coffee.&rdquo; The navigation system will help you find and get directions to a coffee shop, or a coffee shop that sells your favorite kind. Similarly, you could say: &ldquo;Hey, Mercedes, I&rsquo;m too cold.&rdquo; The MBUX system will increase the climate control system temperature to warm the cabin and activate the seat heaters.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EIn addition to the touchscreen and &ldquo;Hey, Mercedes&rdquo; voice prompt, you can interact with MBUX by using touch-sensing buttons on the steering wheel that support scroll, swipe, and select functions. There is a touchpad on the center console, too, complete with handwriting recognition technology.&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003ESome versions have an MBUX Interior Assistant function with movement recognition technology that triggers a predictive response to help make the technology more natural to use.&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EWhat Does Mercedes MBUX Include? - \u003Ca class=\"track-covid-text-links\" href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fquotes.nadaguides.com\u002F?make=Mercedes-Benz&amp;model=cla\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\"\u003EFind the best Mercedes-Benz deals!\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003EMost implementations of MBUX use dual 10.25-inch high-definition displays offering what Mercedes-Benz characterizes as &ldquo;emotional presentations in the form of brilliant graphics.&rdquo; The company is not resorting to hyperbole. Once you&rsquo;ve driven a car or SUV equipped with a high-end version of MBUX, most other modern digital instrumentation and infotainment experiences pale in comparison.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EVehicle owners can alter the instrumentation theme, choosing between Classic, Sport, and Progressive visualizations of information. In AMG models, a Supersport theme is available, along with functions like a race-timer, a G-meter, key engine data, and more.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EEven the most basic versions of MBUX, like what comes standard in the A-Class, include Bluetooth with music streaming, Apple CarPlay, Android Auto, and HD Radio. Depending on the vehicle and equipment, upgrades include Near Field Communication (NFC) Bluetooth pairing, satellite radio, TuneIn radio, a navigation system, and a Wi-Fi hotspot.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EWith navigation, MBUX uses augmented reality technology to help drivers find an address. Using a forward-facing camera, a video view of what&rsquo;s ahead is shown on the infotainment screen, and the augmented reality technology superimposes navigation instructions on the video to show you cross-street names and exactly where you&rsquo;re supposed to turn. Once you&rsquo;re getting close to your destination, this view can also show house and business numbers.&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003ELook for more Mercedes-Benz models to adopt MBUX technology in the future. They&rsquo;ve been around since the late 1950s, when International Harvester introduced the first crew cab truck, and they became popular in the 1990s as Americans increasingly bought pickups to serve as their primary vehicles.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cimg alt=\"Crew Cab Truck 2020 Chevrolet Silverado 1500\" src=\"https:\u002F\u002Fcdn.jdpower.com\u002FJDPA_Crew%20Cab%20Truck%202020%20Chevrolet%20Silverado%201500.jpg\" \u002F\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EToday, crew cab trucks represent the majority of pickups sold in America, and some automakers no longer build the regular-cab trucks that defined the segment for decades.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWhat is a Regular Cab Truck?\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003EA regular-cab truck is a pickup that has a front bench seat, or two individual bucket seats separated by a console. This type of truck can seat one or two people in addition to the driver and offers a small amount of storage space behind the seat. Chevrolet, Ford, GMC, and Ram are the only auto companies that still make regular-cab trucks.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cb\u003EWhat is an Extended Cab Truck?\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003EAn extended-cab truck is a pickup that has the same front seating as a regular-cab truck, but with a small bench seat or jump seats located behind them.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThe rear seating in an extended-cab truck is cramped and best used for children. Adults can ride there for shorter trips, but they won&rsquo;t be very happy about it. Typically, the benefit of an extended-cab truck is the extra covered and locked cargo space they provide behind the front seats. Owners access the space through rear doors that open conventionally or clamshell-style.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EAll of the pickup trucks on sale today come in an extended-cab style, except for the Honda Ridgeline. Chevrolet and GMC call them a Double Cab, Ford calls them a SuperCab, Nissan calls them a King Cab, Ram calls them a Quad Cab, and Toyota calls them an Access Cab.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cb\u003EOther Names for Crew Cab Trucks\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003EIn order to market their trucks in a unique way, some automakers call their crew-cab trucks by a different name. Crew Cab is the most common, but they also go by the names of SuperCrew (Ford), Double Cab (Toyota Tacoma), and CrewMax (Toyota Tundra).\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EAdditionally, Ram sells a version of its Heavy Duty truck called the Mega Cab. A Ram Mega Cab has even more rear seat legroom than the company&rsquo;s Crew Cab models, providing maximum passenger or interior cargo space.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003C\u002Fdiv\u003E\u003Cdiv style='display: inline-block; width: 100%;' class='js-ad-module'\u003E\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cb\u003EHow to Pick the Right Cab When Shopping for a New Truck&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fb\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\u003Cp\u003EChoosing a cab style for a new truck is dependent on several factors. The most obvious pertains to how many people you&rsquo;ll need to carry in the truck. If you&rsquo;re going to carry more than one or two passengers on a regular basis, a regular-cab truck is not going to work.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EAt the same time, light-duty crew-cab trucks are not offered with a long 8-foot cargo bed. They come with regular-length beds and short-length beds. Heavy-duty crew-cab trucks are available with long cargo beds, but they&rsquo;re also more expensive. Therefore, if you&rsquo;re on a tighter budget and need both a long cargo bed and rear seats to carry passengers on occasion, an extended-cab truck might be right for you.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThe reason crew-cab trucks are so popular is because many people buy them for personal rather than professional use. They&rsquo;re used for commuting, for carrying family members, for weekend do-it-yourself projects, and for towing toys to the desert or lake. \u002F\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EGiven that Porsches are synonymous with performance, InnoDrive might seem antithetical to what this proud automaker represents. The image associated with this iconic brand does not always square with the reality. Perhaps you&rsquo;ve noticed that most new Porsches you see on the road are now SUVs of the Cayenne and Macan varieties. And they&rsquo;re frequently driven well within their prodigious limits. Often poorly.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EInnoDrive is for those kinds of Porsche buyers. The people who buy a Porsche because it&rsquo;s a Porsche and not because they want to turn every commute into a slalom run and every drive into a time trial. And let&rsquo;s be honest. In the places where Porsches are popular, like Los Angeles, InnoDrive can help save one&rsquo;s sanity.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EEssentially, Innodrive is an adaptive cruise control system. The technology debuted in the redesigned second-generation \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.jdpower.com\u002Fcars\u002F2020\u002Fporsche\u002Fpanamera\u002Fgts-awd\"\u003EPanamera\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and has since expanded to the redesigned \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.jdpower.com\u002Fcars\u002F2020\u002Fporsche\u002Fcayenne\u002Fawd\"\u003ECayenne SUV\u003C\u002Fa\u003E and \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.jdpower.com\u002Fcars\u002F2020\u002Fporsche\u002F911\u002Fcarrera-coupe\"\u003E911 sports car\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, as well as the \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.jdpower.com\u002Fcars\u002F2020\u002Fporsche\u002Ftaycan\u002Fturbo-sedan\"\u003ETaycan\u003C\u002Fa\u003E electric vehicle. It works like other adaptive cruise control systems to maintain a safe distance from traffic ahead, but InnoDrive is more sophisticated than what you&rsquo;re going to find in something like a \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.jdpower.com\u002Fcars\u002F2020\u002Ftoyota\u002Fcorolla\u002Fle-cvt\"\u003EToyota Corolla\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EFor example, InnoDrive can look up to 1.8 miles ahead on your programmed navigation route and predict when it should accelerate, cruise, coast, and decelerate in order to optimize smoothness and efficiency. The technology takes into account speed limits, elevation changes, curves and corners, and more to determine the optimum powertrain calibration.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EObviously, if you&rsquo;re using a Porsche&rsquo;s adaptive cruise control system, you&rsquo;re more interested in reaching your destination than you are in enjoying the journey. InnoDrive&rsquo;s job is to make the trip as smooth and as seamless as is possible. But the technology can add a bit of a thrill if the driver pushes the Sport button. This automatically changes InnoDrive&rsquo;s character to make the car feel and sound aligned with that mission.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003ETraffic Jam Assist is a part of InnoDrive. During the daily commute, it works at speeds up to 37 mph to maintain safe distances from traffic ahead, follow vehicles as is appropriate, and center the Porsche in the lane of travel. The goal? Stress reduction. So, turn on some Bob Marley and the Wailers and chill, brah. New Audi Connect Generation 3 provides Connect Prime subscribers with basic unlimited Wi-Fi for up to eight devices. Verizon supplies wireless in-vehicle functionality, which includes a new Linux-based operating system, LTE Advanced Pro modem with download speed up to 1 Gbps, 2.4 and 5 GHz bands, and HD voice communication.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003ENew features include a hybrid digital radio, expanded SiriusXM with 360L, a new myAudi app digital storefront, on-demand navigational features, more frequent map updates, Amazon Alexa Auto, and an expanded toll collection module.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EHybrid digital radio comes in handy when traveling outside of a channel&rsquo;s normal range. When the system senses a weak radio signal, the hybrid capability kicks in, picking up the digital feed to ensure a continuous listening experience.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EExpanded SiriusXM with 360L offers upwards of 10,000 hours of on-demand content to its already integrated satellite and streaming service. &ldquo;For You&rdquo; subscribers can discover new content based on existing interests, and readily access college and professional sports, including home and away broadcasts. Customizable profiles for drivers and passengers are stored in the vehicle for added personalization.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThe marketplace accessible through the myAudi app includes several upgrades, such as the ability to purchase in-car features and more flexible subscription plans. Audi Connect Prime and Plus subscribers will enjoy a simplified registration and payment system. Control over smart home devices such as lights, door locks, and garage doors is also available, along with integration of apps that locate and pay for parking. Alexa first launched in the 2019 Audi e-tron SUV and expanded to include many 2020 Audi models. The 2021 Audi A4 and A5 both add Alexa integration.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EWith more and more municipalities moving to electronic tolling, Audi&rsquo;s industry-first integrated toll module (ITM) will expand availability. The ITM allows drivers to adjust the module&rsquo;s setting, including turning it on and off and adjusting for high occupancy vehicle (HOV) lanes. Following on the heels of availability in the 2019 Audi e-tron and \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.jdpower.com\u002Fcars\u002Fexpert-reviews\u002F2020-audi-q7-review?make=audi&amp;model=q7\"\u003E2020 Audi Q7\u003C\u002Fa\u003E, the ITM will launch in most other Audi models.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThese features all complement an already impressive array of capabilities in Audi&rsquo;s MMI.   <script>
   // https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/GlobalEventHandlers/onerror
    window.onerror = function (message, url, lineNumber, column, errorObj) {
        // skipping 'Script error' that doesn't give use any usefull information
        // usually throwed by older browsers
        if (typeof message !== 'undefined' && message.indexOf('Script error.') !== 0) {
            var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            // send errors to clientSideError which will do logger.error
            // and send data to syslog
            xhr.open('POST', '/clientSideError', true);
            xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
            xhr.send('data=' + JSON.stringify({
                message: encodeURIComponent(message),
                fileName: encodeURIComponent(url),
                lineNumber: lineNumber,
                column: column,
                errorObj: errorObj,
                width: document.body.clientWidth || screen.width,
                height: document.body.clientHeight || screen.height,
                useragent: encodeURIComponent(navigator.userAgent),
                url: encodeURIComponent(location.href)
            }));
        }
    };
